Conceptual themes resonate, but the piece reads as a mosaic of strong phrases rather than a fully integrated narrative arc.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=8.0)

  * grade_story_103.txt (grade=7.9)

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=6.8)
    The story’s cohesion depends on its thematic ambition rather than organic integration of elements. Some components (customs office, server hum) feel like mood rather than narrative drivers. The brevity is deliberate but restricts emotional payoff. The chest and fatal flaws anchor the piece, but the spaceport’s broader implications remain underexploited. Lingering questions about legacy and repair suggest depth, but the execution feels prioritized over human relatability.
